class="details-section-contents show-more-container" jscontroller="G7YeLc" jsaction="rcuQ6b:rcuQ6b" data-show-height="144" data-show-use-buffer="true"> <div jscontroller="NlxvWb">  <h1 aria-label=" Description "></h1> <div class="show-more-content text-body" itemprop="description"> <div jsname="C4s9Ed">MX Player - The best way to enjoy your movies.<p><br>a) HARDWARE ACCELERATION - Hardware acceleration can be applied to more videos with the help of new HW+ decoder.<p>b) MULTI-CORE DECODING - MX Player is the first Android video player which supports multi-core decoding. Test result proved that dual-core device’s performance is up to 70% better than single-core devices.<p>c) PINCH TO ZOOM, ZOOM AND PAN - Easily zoom in and out by pinching and swiping across the screen. Zoom and Pan is also available by option.<p>d) SUBTITLE GESTURES - Scroll forward/backward to move to next/previous text, Up/down to move text up and down, Zoom in/out to change text size.<p>e) KIDS LOCK - Keep your kids entertained without having to worry that they can make calls or touch other apps. (plugin required)<p><br>Subtitle formats:<p>- DVD, DVB, SSA/ASS Subtitle tracks.<br>- SubStation Alpha(.ssa/.ass) with full styling.<br>- SAMI(.smi) with ruby tag support.<br>- SubRip(.srt)<br>- MicroDVD(.sub)<br>- VobSub(.sub/.idx)<br>- SubViewer2.0(.sub)<br>- MPL2(.mpl)<br>- TMPlayer(.txt)<br>- Teletext<br>- PJS(.pjs)<br>- WebVTT(.vtt)<p>******<br>About &quot;Draw over other apps&quot; permission: This permission is required to block system buttons when input blocking is activated on the playback screen.<br>About &quot;Control vibration&quot;, &quot;Prevent phone from sleeping&quot; permissions: These permissions are required for media playback on some devices.<br>******<br>If you are facing &quot;package file is invalid&quot; error, please install it again from product home page (<a href="https://www.google.com/url?q=https://www.google.com/url?q%3Dhttps://sites.google.com/site/mxvpen/download%26sa%3DD%26usg%3DAFQjCNFVy6-l6Iow2-l-YwxNChmw6F66Cw&amp;sa=D&amp;usg=AFQjCNGr0975shUpiXfZycayKjh5ST22lQ" target="_blank">https://sites.google.com/site/mxvpen/download</a>)<br>******<p><br>If you have any questions, please visit XDA MX Player forum.<br><a href="https://www.google.com/url?q=https://www.google.com/url?q%3Dhttp://forum.xda-developers.com/apps/mx-player%26sa%3DD%26usg%3DAFQjCNGUFBQxEmvOIdAm3TKlz-ZzUb2nzg&amp;sa=D&amp;usg=AFQjCNGsCQorCSmzbyVYl_GO6bUEHXnD9w" target="_blank">http://forum.xda-developers.com/apps/mx-player</a><p>Some of the screens are from the Elephants Dreams licensed under the Creative Commons Attribution 2.5.<br>(c) copyright 2006,
